\usemodule

\definebodyfontenvironment

\setupGNUPLOTterminal

    dashed=yes, % *yes* | no
    dashlength=2, % scaling factor for dash lengths
    linewidth=2, % scaling factor for line widths (1.0 means 0.5bp)
    %fontscale=1, % scaling factor for text labels
